  <section class="section grey-bg what-is-cbd">
   <div class="container">
    <h2 class="section__title">
     <span>
      What is
     </span>
     CBD Oil?
    </h2>
    <div class="what-is-cbd__left-col">
     <p>
      CBD is a chemical compound of marijuana that has no properties which affect the mind negatively. Insead, it has many medicinal features. In this section, we will talk about how cannabidiol can alleviate and diminish the symptoms of menacing diseases and assist in their cure.
     </p>
     <div class="what-is-cbd__right-col">
      <p>
       Cannabidiol (CBD) is contained in marijuana on a par with tetrahydrocannabinol (THC) and other 113 matters. The most notable characteristics of CBD is that its use is not associated with alterations in brain functions, such as consciousness and perception. However, during the process of cannabis consumption, CBD allows you to relax the body and eliminate abrupt onsets of intense fear or discomfort. The compound is identified in the cannabis plant while it’s blooming and is most frequently made by pressing its seeds to derive the fatty oils from them.
      </p>
      <p>
       The main parts of the human body which cannabidiol impacts are CB1 receptors that are located in the nervous system, and CB2 receptors. The THC, which is always found in cannabis, activates the work of these receptors, resulting in the effect of “getting high” while smoking. Whereas CBD is a harmless compound which restrains receptors while eliminating the adverse effects of marijuana.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="what-is-cbd__img rocket-lazyload" data-bg="https://validcbdoil.com/wp-content/themes/validcbdoil/img/what-is-sbd-bg.png" style="">
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="point">
    </div>
   </div>
  </section>
  <section class="section classified-section">
   <div class="container">
    <div class="classified-section__title-container">
     <h2 class="section__title">
      CBD can be
      <span>
       classified into
      </span>
     </h2>
    </div>
    <div class="flex-column flex-lg-row justify-content-lg-between">
     <div class="classified-section__item">
      <h4 class="title">
       Full spectrum
      </h4>
      <p>
       But what’s the difference between them? The first type denotes pure CBD oil derived from hemp that has all the composites contained in the cannabis plant. This type of oil is entirely pure and includes a wide range of essential minerals, vitamins, proteins, fatty acids, chlorophyll, terpenes, flavonoids and fibers. There is a 90% cannabidiol concentration in the total full spectrum CBD mass. If you use full spectrum CBD oil, you will benefit greatly from the effect.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="classified-section__item">
      <h4 class="title">
       CBD isolate
      </h4>
      <p>
       CBD isolate is a crystalline form of the hemp oil. CBD in the form of crystals is separated from other cannabinoids found in cannabis. The obtained substance is derived mostly from cannabis plant, therefore bringing CBD in its purest form. It is then cleaned and cooled to get rid of excess wax. The final product is a snow-white powder that contains 99% of pure Cannabidiol. Besides, products containing CBD compound are defined as 99% pure due to the fact that CBD exists separately from other compounds.
      </p>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>
  </section>
  <section class="section benefits-section main-page grey-bg">
   <div class="container">
    <div class="section__header">
     <h2 class="section__title">
      Benefits
      <span>
       of
      </span>
      CBD Oil
     </h2>
     <p>
      At present, CBD oil has a plethora of benefits for the human body that can make a decent contribution to health betterment. Catch up with us to know about the most useful properties of a substance.
     </p>
    </div>
    <div class="benefits-section__bg">
     <div class="benefits-section__item">
      <h3 class="title">
       Fights against emotional impairment
      </h3>
      <p>
       CBD narrows major symptoms of a long- term mental disorder (schizophrenia) and other associated disorders.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="benefits-section__item">
      <h3 class="title">
       Oils are Guardians of Cancer Development
      </h3>
      <p>
       They found that CBD helps reduce harmful cells in swollen tissues by regulating and decreasing the rapid growth of cancer cells.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="benefits-section__item">
      <h3 class="title">
       Helps prevent digestive dysfunction
      </h3>
      <p>
       The human body is prone to suffering physically both from external and internal injuries after traumas and illnesses. In such cases, the stomach needs lots of nutrients that contain useful vitamins and minerals
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="benefits-section__item">
      <h3 class="title">
       Helps to diminish pain
      </h3>
      <p>
       It functions as a painkiller, triggering pain and relieving it. It also acts as a drug that reduces inflammation and swelling.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="benefits-section__item">
      <h3 class="title">
       CBD Hemp Oil Subdues Anxiety
      </h3>
      <p>
       CBD oil can minimize serious signs of social anxiety
      </p>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>
  </section>
  <section class="section side-effect">
   <div class="container">
    <div class="section__header">
     <h2 class="section__title">
      <span>
       CBD Oil
      </span>
      Side Effects
     </h2>
     <p>
      Despite the many above-mentioned advantages of using CBD, there are also variouscside effects that can impact the human body from the negative perspective. Although they are insignificant and do not pose tremendous harm to an organism, it is important to remember that the influence of CBD oil affects everyone individually, and what may happen to one person does not necessarily mean that it will happen to you too.
     </p>
     <p>
      Therefore, it is important to start taking CBD very carefully and consciously. Start with a moderate dose and increase it little by little. In case the least side effects are noticeable, reduce the dose or stop using the substance.
     </p>
    </div>
    <div class="flex-column flex-lg-row">
     <div class="side-effect__item">
      <h3 class="green-marijuana-title">
       Dry mouth
      </h3>
      <p>
       Despite the fact that the likelihood of this side effect is quite low, CBD can cause intense thirst. This is the number one adverse effect of using cannabis CBD oil which is not severe, yet unpleasant, especially for those who try CBD for the first time.
      </p>
      <p>
       It occurs because submaxillary glands – the most active organs that produce saliva – secrete it in much lesser concentrations. Consequently, while the cannabis compound is being taken, essential lubrication is not produced. This, in turn, leads to excessive dryness, along with the feeling of great discomfort in mouth cavity.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="side-effect__item">
      <h3 class="green-marijuana-title">
       Lower blood pressure
      </h3>
      <p>
       Once CBD oil is consumed in doses that exceed prescribed ones, a slight decrease in the speed of blood pushing against the walls of arteries becomes one of potential side effects of hemp CBD oil consumption. This symptom is, as a rule, not long-lasting.
      </p>
      <p>
       Also, please note that CBD intake is strictly prohibited in cases when blood pressure medications are taken. If you belong to such people, it’s essential to consider recommendations from doctor before buying any CBD product.
      </p>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="flex-column flex-lg-row">
     <div class="side-effect__item">
      <h3 class="green-marijuana-title">
       Increased involuntary quivering movements in patients with Parkinson’s disease
      </h3>
      <p>
       Despite the fact that the likelihood of this side effect is quite low, CBD can cause intense thirst. This is the number one adverse effect of using cannabis CBD oil which is not severe, yet unpleasant, especially for those who try CBD for the first time.
      </p>
      <p>
       It occurs because submaxillary glands – the most active organs that produce saliva – secrete it in much lesser concentrations. Consequently, while the cannabis compound is being taken, essential lubrication is not produced. This, in turn, leads to excessive dryness, along with the feeling of great discomfort in mouth cavity.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="side-effect__item">
      <div>
       <h3 class="green-marijuana-title">
        Sleepiness
       </h3>
       <p>
        Other scientific research shows that CBD is an eugeroic (a drug that fosters wakefulness and alertness). But whenever used in doses that exceed the norm, CBD can impact people differently and mostly lead to a feeling of being sleepy and lethargic. If you experience this side effect, do not drive any vehicles; the best way out in this case is to lower the dose you take normally until the signs of ailment disappear completely.
       </p>
      </div>
      <div>
       <h3 class="green-marijuana-title">
        Dizziness
       </h3>
       <p>
        This ailment is most frequently a result of a decrease in blood pressure. This condition takes place when a person takes big doses of CBD. However, this effect doesn’t last for long and can usually be eliminated with a cup of tea or coffee.
       </p>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="section__header mb-0">
     <p>
      There are both benefits and negative impacts of CBD oil intake that can influence your health either from the good side or from the bad one. However, the latter case can happen only if you don’t follow the instructions and neglect the acceptable dosage. Either way, CBD extract available in oils has a great potential to decrease negative processes in the human body and liquidate the symptoms of many diseases if taken carefully.
     </p>
    </div>
   </div>
  </section>

  <script>
   jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
        const firstColumn           = $('#first-calc-column'),
            secondColumn          = $('#second-calc-column'),
            calcBanner            = $('#calc-block-banner'),
            bannerTitle           = calcBanner.find('.banner-block__title span'),
            bannerSubTitle        = calcBanner.find('.banner-block__subtitle'),
            board                 = calcBanner.find('.banner-block__board'),
            boardDescription      = board.find('.board-description'),
            boardLogotype         = board.find('.board-logo'),
            boardLink             = board.find('.board-link');

        firstColumn.find('.calc-list .calc-list__item').on('click', function () {
            const _this = $(this);
            const position = _this.attr('data-position');

            const promise = new Promise(resolve => {
                _this.prevAll().removeClass('active');
                _this.nextAll().removeClass('active');
                _this.addClass('active');

                resolve();
            })

            promise
                .then(()=>{
                    secondColumn.find('.calc-list.active').removeClass('active');
                })
                .then(()=> {
                    secondColumn.find(`.calc-list[data-position="${position}"]`).addClass('active');
                })
                .then(()=>{
                    secondColumn.find(`.calc-list[data-position="${position}"] .calc-list__item`).removeClass('active');
                })
                .then(()=>{
                    const _thisButton = secondColumn.find(`.calc-list[data-position="${position}"] .calc-list__item:first-child`),
                        grams = _thisButton.attr('data-grams'),
                        title = _thisButton.attr('data-title'),
                        description = _thisButton.attr('data-description'),
                        logo = _thisButton.attr('data-logo'),
                        link = _thisButton.attr('data-link');

                    bannerTitle.text(grams);
                    bannerSubTitle.text(title);
                    boardDescription.text(description);
                    boardLogotype.attr('src', logo);
                    boardLink.attr('href', link);
                    _thisButton.addClass('active');
                })

        });

        secondColumn.find('.calc-list .calc-list__item').on('click', function () {
            const _this = $(this),
                grams = _this.attr('data-grams'),
                title = _this.attr('data-title'),
                description = _this.attr('data-description'),
                logo = _this.attr('data-logo'),
                link = _this.attr('data-link');

            const promise = new Promise(resolve => {
                _this.prevAll().removeClass('active');
                _this.nextAll().removeClass('active');
                _this.addClass('active');

                resolve();
            })

            promise.then(()=>{
                bannerTitle.text(grams);
                bannerSubTitle.text(title);
                boardDescription.text(description);
                boardLogotype.attr('src', logo);
                boardLink.attr('href', link);
            })
        });
    });
  </script>

  <section class="section faq-section">
   <div class="container">
    <div class="section__header">
     <h2 class="section__title">
      FAQ
     </h2>
     <p>
      If you’re still on the fence about buying the best CBD oil, consider these points before embarking on the right option.
     </p>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-accordion">
     <details class="item">
      <summary>
       How to Store CBD oil?
      </summary>
      <div>
       <p>
        Best organic CBD oil should be stored in a dry and cool place. In particular, CBD oils should be kept away from heat and light sources in order to preserve their contents. We recommend storing the products in their original packaging.
       </p>
      </div>
     </details>
     <details class="item">
      <summary>
       Does CBD production imply animal testings?
      </summary>
      <div>
       <p>
        No. CBD is 100% vegetarian and organically synthesized by plants.
       </p>
      </div>
     </details>
     <details class="item">
      <summary>
       How long does it take for CBD oil to bring visible effects?
      </summary>
      <div>
       <p>
        At the optimal dosage, it normally takes from 20 to 30 minutes for the CBD effects to be noticeable. Considering that CBD is deprived of any psychoactive components, you can’t get high while taking it. You may feel less pain, reduced tremor, and increased composure. The general effects depend on the reasons why you are consuming CBD oil, whether you are adhering to the right dosage to fight your symptoms, and whether CBD has any effect on you.
       </p>
      </div>
     </details>
     <details class="item">
      <summary>
       How can I calculate the right CBD oil dosage?
      </summary>
      <div>
       <p>
        Everything depends on the effect you want to achieve by using the oil, and, of course, your weight parameters. For example, if you weigh less than 130 pounds and want to experience slight CBD oil effects, 11 mg for each dose will be more than enough. This is to take into account 40 doses per 450-mg bottle potency. On the contrary, if your weight 230 pounds or more and wish to feel strong effects, the same potency will be sufficient for approximately 10 doses.
       </p>
      </div>
     </details>
     <details class="item">
      <summary>
       Does your job require any drug testings?
      </summary>
      <div>
       <p>
        If yes, we highly recommend not to go for full spectrum CBD oil which contains some concentration of THC. As an alternative, you can use crystalline isolate oils. These do not contain THC whatsoever, which can help you pass the drug test successfully.
       </p>
      </div>
     </details>
    </div>
   </div>
